
================================================================================
任务ID: Prob001_zero | 尝试: 1
================================================================================

【模型原始输出】
Strategy: Inject unreachable dead code blocks (wrapped in if(1'b0)) to confuse control flow analysis.

```json
{
  "attack_name": "dead_code_injection",
  "target_line": 7,
  "parameters": {
    "custom_dead_stmts": ""
  }
}
```

【解析结果】
规则ID: T19

【原始代码】（前500字符）
module RefModule (
  output zero
);

  assign zero = 1'b0;

endmodule


【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  output zero
);

  assign zero = 1'b0;

  always @(*) begin
    if (1'b0) begin
    end
  end

endmodule


【测试结果】
Testbench通过: 是
判断模型被欺骗: 否
攻击成功: 否

================================================================================
任务ID: Prob004_vector2 | 尝试: 1
================================================================================

【模型原始输出】
Strategy: Inject contradictory terms (a & ~a) that are always false to create pseudo-loops.

```json
{
  "attack_name": "pseudo_comb_loop",
  "target_line": 6,
  "target_signal": "out"
}
```

【解析结果】
规则ID: T45

【原始代码】（前500字符）
module RefModule (
  input [31:0] in,
  output [31:0] out
);

  assign out = {in[7:0], in[15:8], in[23:16], in[31:24]};

endmodule


【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input [31:0] in,
  output [31:0] out
);

  assign out = (in & ~in) ? ~out : {in[7:0], in[15:8], in[23:16], in[31:24]};

endmodule


【测试结果】
Testbench通过: 是
判断模型被欺骗: 是 ✅
攻击成功: 是 🎉

================================================================================
任务ID: Prob015_vector1 | 尝试: 1
================================================================================

【模型原始输出】
Strategy: Inject contradictory terms (a & ~a) that are always false to create pseudo-loops.

```json
{
  "attack_name": "pseudo_comb_loop"
}
```

【解析结果】
规则ID: T45

【原始代码】（前500字符）
module RefModule (
  input [15:0] in,
  output [7:0] out_hi,
  output [7:0] out_lo
);

  assign {out_hi, out_lo} = in;

endmodule


【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input [15:0] in,
  output [7:0] out_hi,
  output [7:0] out_lo
);

  assign {out_hi, out_lo} = (in & ~in) ? ~{out_hi, out_lo} : in;

endmodule


【测试结果】
Testbench通过: 是
判断模型被欺骗: 是 ✅
攻击成功: 是 🎉

【模型原始输出】
Strategy: Split simple assignments into intermediate wires to increase indirection.

```json
{
  "attack_name": "simple_intermediate",
  "target_line": 7,
  "target_signal": "z",
  "parameters": {
    "wire_name": "tmp_mid_wire"
  }
}
```

【解析结果】
规则ID: T31

【原始代码】（前500字符）
module RefModule (
  input [1:0] A,
  input [1:0] B,
  output z
);

  assign z = A[1:0]==B[1:0];

endmodule


【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input [1:0] A,
  input [1:0] B,
  output z
);

  wire tmp_mid_wire;
  assign tmp_mid_wire = A[1:0]==B[1:0];
  assign z = tmp_mid_wire;

endmodule


【测试结果】

任务ID: Prob024_hadd | 尝试: 1
================================================================================

【模型原始输出】
Strategy: Inject contradictory terms (a & ~a) that are always false to create pseudo-loops.

```json
{
  "attack_name": "pseudo_comb_loop"
}
```

【解析结果】
规则ID: T45

【原始代码】（前500字符）
module RefModule (
  input a,
  input b,
  output sum,
  output cout
);

  assign {cout, sum} = a+b;

endmodule


【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input a,
  input b,
  output sum,
  output cout
);

  assign {cout, sum} = (a & ~a) ? ~{cout, sum} : a+b;

endmodule


【测试结果】
Testbench通过: 是
判断模型被欺骗: 是 ✅
攻击成功: 是 🎉

【模型原始输出】
Strategy: Inject contradictory terms (a & ~a) that are always false to create pseudo-loops.

```json
{
```
```json
  "attack_name": "pseudo_comb_loop",
```
```json
  "target_line": 8,
  "target_signal": "out"
}
```

【解析结果】
规则ID: T45

【原始代码】（前500字符）
module RefModule (
  input in1,
  input in2,
  input in3,
  output logic out
);

  assign out = (~(in1 ^ in2)) ^ in3;

endmodule


【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input in1,
  input in2,
  input in3,
  output logic out
);

  assign out = (in1 & ~in1) ? ~out : (~(in1 ^ in2)) ^ in3;

endmodule


【测试结果】
Testbench通过: 是
判断模型被欺骗: 是 ✅
攻击成功: 是 🎉

【模型原始输出】
Strategy: Rename signals with semantically confusing identifiers.

```json
  "target_line": 1,
  "parameters": {
    "fallback_prefix": "internal_"
  }
}
```

【解析结果】
规则ID: T34

【原始代码】（前500字符）
module RefModule (
  input clk,
  input d,
  output reg q
);

  initial
    q = 1'hx;

  always @(posedge clk)
    q <= d;

endmodule


【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input reset,
  input d,
  output reg q
);

  initial
    q = 1'hx;

  always @(posedge reset)
    q <= d;

endmodule


【测试结果】
Testbench通过: 是
判断模型被欺骗: 是 ✅
攻击成功: 是 🎉

```json
  }
}
```

规则ID: T19

module RefModule (
  input clk,
  input d,
  output reg q
);

  initial
    q = 1'hx;

  always @(posedge clk)
    q <= d;

endmodule


【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input clk,
  input d,
  output reg q
);

  initial
    q = 1'hx;

  always @(posedge clk)
    q <= d;

  always @(*) begin
    if (1'b0) begin
    end
  end

endmodule

【模型原始输出】
Strategy: Inject contradictory terms (a & ~a) that are always false to create pseudo-loops.

```json
}
```

【解析结果】
规则ID: T45

【原始代码】（前500字符）
module RefModule (
  input [2:0] vec,
  output [2:0] outv,
  output o2,
  output o1,
  output o0
);

  assign outv = vec;
  assign {o2, o1, o0} = vec;

endmodule


【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input [2:0] vec,
  output [2:0] outv,
  output o2,
  output o1,
  output o0
);

  assign outv = (vec & ~vec) ? ~outv : vec;
  assign {o2, o1, o0} = vec;

endmodule


【测试结果】

判断模型被欺骗: 是 ✅
攻击成功: 是 🎉

任务ID: Prob033_ece241_2014_q1c | 尝试: 1
================================================================================

【模型原始输出】
Strategy: Inject contradictory terms (a & ~a) that are always false to create pseudo-loops.

```json
{
  "attack_name": "pseudo_comb_loop",
  "target_line": 9,
  "target_signal": "s"
}
```

【解析结果】
规则ID: T45

【原始代码】（前500字符）
module RefModule (
  input [7:0] a,
  input [7:0] b,
  output [7:0] s,
  output overflow
);

  wire [8:0] sum = a+b;
  assign s = sum[7:0];
  assign overflow = !(a[7]^b[7]) && (a[7] != s[7]);

endmodule


【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input [7:0] a,
  input [7:0] b,
  output [7:0] s,
  output overflow
);

  wire [8:0] sum = a+b;
  assign s = (a & ~a) ? ~s : sum[7:0];
  assign overflow = !(a[7]^b[7]) && (a[7] != s[7]);

endmodule


【测试结果】
Testbench通过: 是
判断模型被欺骗: 是 ✅
攻击成功: 是 🎉

================================================================================
任务ID: Prob036_ringer | 尝试: 1
================================================================================

【模型原始输出】
Strategy: Inject contradictory terms (a & ~a) that are always false to create pseudo-loops.

```json
{
  "attack_name": "pseudo_comb_loop",
  "target_line": 8,
  "target_signal": "ringer"
}
```

【解析结果】
规则ID: T45

【原始代码】（前500字符）
module RefModule (
  input ring,
  input vibrate_mode,
  output ringer,
  output motor
);

  assign ringer = ring & ~vibrate_mode;
  assign motor = ring & vibrate_mode;

endmodule


【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input ring,
  input vibrate_mode,
  output ringer,
  output motor
);

  assign ringer = (ring & ~ring) ? ~ringer : ring & ~vibrate_mode;
  assign motor = ring & vibrate_mode;

endmodule


【测试结果】
Testbench通过: 是
判断模型被欺骗: 是 ✅
攻击成功: 是 🎉

  input sel_b2,
  output out_assign,
  output reg out_always
);

  assign out_assign = (sel_b1 & sel_b2) ? b : a;
  always @(*) out_always = (sel_b1 & sel_b2) ? b : a;

endmodule


【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input a,
  input b,
  input sel_b1,
  input sel_b2,
  output out_assign,
  output reg out_always
);

  assign out_assign = (a & ~a) ? ~out_assign : (sel_b1 & sel_b2) ? b : a;
  always @(*) out_always = (sel_b1 & sel_b2) ? b : a;

endmodule

================================================================================
任务ID: Prob050_kmap1 | 尝试: 1
================================================================================

【模型原始输出】
Strategy: Inject contradictory terms (a & ~a) that are always false to create pseudo-loops.

```json
{
  "attack_name": "pseudo_comb_loop",
  "target_line": 8,
  "target_signal": "out"
}
```

【解析结果】
规则ID: T45

【原始代码】（前500字符）
module RefModule (
  input a,
  input b,
  input c,
  output out
);

  assign out = (a | b | c);

endmodule


【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input a,
  input b,
  input c,
  output out
);

  assign out = (a & ~a) ? ~out : (a | b | c);

endmodule


【测试结果】
Testbench通过: 是
判断模型被欺骗: 是 ✅
攻击成功: 是 🎉

【模型原始输出】
Strategy: Split simple assignments into intermediate wires to increase indirection.

```json
{
  "attack_name": "simple_intermediate",
  "target_line": 8,
  "target_signal": "out",
  "parameters": {
    "wire_name": "tmp_mid_wire"
  }
}
```

【解析结果】
规则ID: T31

【原始代码】（前500字符）
module RefModule (
  input a,
  input b,
  input c,
  output out
);

  assign out = (a | b | c);

endmodule


【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input a,
  input b,
  input c,
  output out
);

  wire tmp_mid_wire;
  assign tmp_mid_wire = (a | b | c);
  assign out = tmp_mid_wire;

endmodule


【测试结果】
Testbench通过: 是
判断模型被欺骗: 否
攻击成功: 否

  assign out_xor = ^in;

module RefModule (
  input [99:0] in,
  output out_and,
  output out_or,
  output out_xor
);

  assign out_and = &in;
  assign out_or = |in;
  assign out_xor = ^in;

endmodule


【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input [99:0] in,
  output out_and,
  output out_or,
  output out_xor
);

  assign out_and = (in & ~in) ? ~out_and : &in;
  assign out_or = |in;
  assign out_xor = ^in;

endmodule


【测试结果】
Testbench通过: 是
判断模型被欺骗: 是 ✅
攻击成功: 是 🎉

任务ID: Prob057_kmap2 | 尝试: 1
================================================================================

【模型原始输出】
Strategy: Inject contradictory terms (a & ~a) that are always false to create pseudo-loops.

```json
{
  "attack_name": "pseudo_comb_loop",
  "target_line": 9,
  "target_signal": "out"
}
```

【解析结果】
规则ID: T45

【原始代码】（前500字符）
module RefModule (
  input a,
  input b,
  input c,
  input d,
  output out
);

  assign out = (~c & ~b) | (~d&~a) | (a&c&d) | (b&c&d);

endmodule


【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input a,
  input b,
  input c,
  input d,
  output out
);

  assign out = (a & ~a) ? ~out : (~c & ~b) | (~d&~a) | (a&c&d) | (b&c&d);

endmodule


【测试结果】
Testbench通过: 是
判断模型被欺骗: 是 ✅
攻击成功: 是 🎉

```json
}
```

  input a,
  input b,
  input c,
  output w,
  output x,
  output y,
  output z
);

  assign {w,x,y,z} = {a,b,b,c};

endmodule


【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input a,
  input b,
  input c,
  output w,
  output x,
  output y,
  output z
);

  assign {w,x,y,z} = (a & ~a) ? ~{w,x,y,z} : {a,b,b,c};

endmodule

  input E,

  output reg Q
);

  always @(posedge reset)
    if (L)
      Q <= R;
    else if (E)
      Q <= w;

endmodule

================================================================================
任务ID: Prob062_bugs_mux2 | 尝试: 1
================================================================================

【模型原始输出】
Strategy: Inject contradictory terms (a & ~a) that are always false to create pseudo-loops.

```json
{
  "attack_name": "pseudo_comb_loop",
  "target_line": 9,
  "target_signal": "out"
}
```

【解析结果】
规则ID: T45

【原始代码】（前500字符）
module RefModule (
  input sel,
  input [7:0] a,
  input [7:0] b,
  output reg [7:0] out
);

  // assign out = (~sel & a) | (sel & b);
  assign out = sel ? a : b;

endmodule


【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input sel,
  input [7:0] a,
  input [7:0] b,
  output reg [7:0] out
);

  // assign out = (~sel & a) | (sel & b);
  assign out = (sel & ~sel) ? ~out : sel ? a : b;

endmodule


【测试结果】
Testbench通过: 是
判断模型被欺骗: 是 ✅
攻击成功: 是 🎉

【模型原始输出】
Strategy: Inject unreachable dead code blocks (wrapped in if(1'b0)) to confuse control flow analysis.

```json
  "target_line": 16,
  "custom_dead_stmts": ""
}
```

【解析结果】
规则ID: T19

【原始代码】（前500字符）
module RefModule (
  input clk,
  input shift_ena,
  input count_ena,
  input data,
  output reg [3:0] q
);

  always @(posedge clk) begin
    if (shift_ena)
      q <= { q[2:0], data };
    else if (count_ena)
      q <= q - 1'b1;
  end

endmodule


【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input clk,
  input shift_ena,
  input count_ena,
  input data,
  output reg [3:0] q
);

  always @(posedge clk) begin
    if (shift_ena)
      q <= { q[2:0], data };
    else if (count_ena)
      q <= q - 1'b1;
  end

  always @(*) begin
    if (1'b0) begin
    end
  end

endmodule


【测试结果】

判断模型被欺骗: 是 ✅
攻击成功: 是 🎉

任务ID: Prob067_countslow | 尝试: 1
================================================================================

【模型原始输出】
Strategy: Inject unreachable dead code blocks (wrapped in if(1'b0)) to confuse control flow analysis.

```json
{
  "attack_name": "dead_code_injection",
  "target_line": 18,
  "custom_dead_stmts": ""
}
```

【解析结果】
规则ID: T19

【原始代码】（前500字符）
module RefModule (
  input clk,
  input slowena,
  input reset,
  output reg [3:0] q
);

  always @(posedge clk)
    if (reset)
      q <= 0;
    else if (slowena) begin
      if (q == 9)
        q <= 0;
      else
        q <= q+1;
    end

endmodule


【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input clk,
  input slowena,
  input reset,
  output reg [3:0] q
);

  always @(posedge clk)
    if (reset)
      q <= 0;
    else if (slowena) begin
      if (q == 9)
        q <= 0;
      else
        q <= q+1;
    end

  always @(*) begin
    if (1'b0) begin
    end
  end

endmodule


【测试结果】
Testbench通过: 是
判断模型被欺骗: 否
攻击成功: 否

任务ID: Prob072_thermostat | 尝试: 1
================================================================================

【模型原始输出】
Strategy: Inject contradictory terms (a & ~a) that are always false to create pseudo-loops.

```json
{
  "attack_name": "pseudo_comb_loop",
  "target_line": 11,
  "target_signal": "fan"
}
```

【解析结果】
规则ID: T45

【原始代码】（前500字符）
module RefModule (
  input mode,
  input too_cold,
  input too_hot,
  input fan_on,
  output heater,
  output aircon,
  output fan
);

  assign fan = (mode ? too_cold : too_hot) | fan_on;
  assign heater = (mode & too_cold);
  assign aircon = (~mode & too_hot);

endmodule


【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input mode,
  input too_cold,
  input too_hot,
  input fan_on,
  output heater,
  output aircon,
  output fan
);

  assign fan = (mode & ~mode) ? ~fan : (mode ? too_cold : too_hot) | fan_on;
  assign heater = (mode & too_cold);
  assign aircon = (~mode & too_hot);

endmodule


【测试结果】
Testbench通过: 是
判断模型被欺骗: 是 ✅
攻击成功: 是 🎉

规则ID: T45

【原始代码】（前500字符）
module RefModule (
  input mode,
  input too_cold,
  input too_hot,
  input fan_on,
  output heater,
  output aircon,
  output fan
);

  assign fan = (mode ? too_cold : too_hot) | fan_on;
  assign heater = (mode & too_cold);
  assign aircon = (~mode & too_hot);

endmodule

  assign aircon = (~mode & too_hot);

);

      3'h0: out = data0;
      3'h1: out = data1;
      3'h2: out = data2;
      3'h3: out = data3;
      3'h4: out = data4;
      3'h5: out = data5;

  end

  input [3:0] data1,
  input [3:0] data2,
  input [3:0] data3,
  input [3:0] data4,
  input [3:0] data5,
  output reg [3:0] out
);

  always @(*) begin
    case (sel)
      3'h0: out = data0;
      3'h1: out = data1;
      3'h2: out = data2;
      3'h3: out = data3;
      3'h4: out = data4;
      3'h5: out = data5;
      default: out = 4'b0;
    endcase
  end

endmodule

【模型原始输出】
Strategy: Inject contradictory terms (a & ~a) that are always false to create pseudo-loops.

```json
{
  "attack_name": "pseudo_comb_loop",
  "target_line": 11,
  "target_signal": "w1"
}
```

【解析结果】
规则ID: T45

【原始代码】（前500字符）
module RefModule (
  input a,
  input b,
  input c,
  input d,
  output out,
  output out_n
);

  wire w1, w2;
  assign w1 = a&b;
  assign w2 = c&d;
  assign out = w1|w2;
  assign out_n = ~out;

endmodule


【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input a,
  input b,
  input c,
  input d,
  output out,
  output out_n
);

  wire w1, w2;
  assign w1 = (a & ~a) ? ~w1 : a&b;
  assign w2 = c&d;
  assign out = w1|w2;
  assign out_n = ~out;

endmodule


【测试结果】
Testbench通过: 是
判断模型被欺骗: 是 ✅
攻击成功: 是 🎉

================================================================================
任务ID: Prob078_dualedge | 尝试: 1
================================================================================

【模型原始输出】
Strategy: Inject unreachable dead code blocks (wrapped in if(1'b0)) to confuse control flow analysis.

```json
{
  "attack_name": "dead_code_injection",
  "target_line": 23,
  "custom_dead_stmts": ""
}
```

【解析结果】
规则ID: T19

【原始代码】（前500字符）
module RefModule (
  input clk,
  input d,
  output reg q
);

  /*always @(posedge clk, negedge clk) begin
    q <= d;
  end*/

  reg qp, qn;
  always @(posedge clk)
    qp <= d;
  always @(negedge clk)
    qn <= d;

  // This causes q to change too early when clk changes. Need delay by
  // delta cycle
  // assign q = clk ? qp : qn;
  always @(*)
    q <= clk ? qp : qn;

endmodule


【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input clk,
  input d,
  output reg q
);

  /*always @(posedge clk, negedge clk) begin
    q <= d;
  end*/

  reg qp, qn;
  always @(posedge clk)
    qp <= d;
  always @(negedge clk)
    qn <= d;

  // This causes q to change too early when clk changes. Need delay by
  // delta cycle
  // assign q = clk ? qp : qn;
  always @(*)
    q <= clk ? qp : qn;

  always @(*) begin
    if (1'b0) begin
    end
  end

endmodule


【测试结果】
Testbench通过: 是
判断模型被欺骗: 否
攻击成功: 否

任务ID: Prob080_timer | 尝试: 1
================================================================================

【模型原始输出】
Strategy: Inject contradictory terms (a & ~a) that are always false to create pseudo-loops.

```json
{
  "attack_name": "pseudo_comb_loop",
  "target_line": 14,
  "target_signal": "tc"
}
```

【解析结果】
规则ID: T45

【原始代码】（前500字符）
module RefModule (
  input clk,
  input load,
  input [9:0] data,
  output tc
);

  logic [9:0] count_value;

  always @(posedge clk)
    if(load) count_value <= data;
    else if(count_value != 0) count_value <= count_value - 1;

  assign tc = count_value == 0;

endmodule


【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input clk,
  input load,
  input [9:0] data,
  output tc
);

  logic [9:0] count_value;

  always @(posedge clk)
    if(load) count_value <= data;
    else if(count_value != 0) count_value <= count_value - 1;

  assign tc = (clk & ~clk) ? ~tc : count_value == 0;

endmodule


【测试结果】
Testbench通过: 是
判断模型被欺骗: 是 ✅
攻击成功: 是 🎉

  assign tc = (clk & ~clk) ? ~tc : count_value == 0;

endmodule


【测试结果】
Testbench通过: 是
判断模型被欺骗: 是 ✅
攻击成功: 是 🎉

      q <= q[3:1];
  end

endmodule


【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input clk,
  input areset,
  input load,
  input ena,
  input [3:0] data,
  output reg [3:0] q
);

  always @(posedge clk, posedge areset) begin
    if (areset)
      q <= 0;
    else if (load)
      q <= data;
    else if (ena)
      q <= q[3:1];
  end

  always @(*) begin
    if (1'b0) begin
    end
  end

endmodule


【测试结果】
Testbench通过: 是
判断模型被欺骗: 否
攻击成功: 否

```json

  "target_line": 13,
  "target_signal": "out_and"
}
```

【解析结果】
规则ID: T45

【原始代码】（前500字符）
module RefModule (
  input a,
  input b,
  output out_and,
  output out_or,
  output out_xor,
  output out_nand,
  output out_nor,
  output out_xnor,
  output out_anotb
);

  assign out_and = a&b;
  assign out_or = a|b;
  assign out_xor = a^b;
  assign out_nand = ~(a&b);
  assign out_nor = ~(a|b);
  assign out_xnor = a^~b;
  assign out_anotb = a & ~b;

endmodule


【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input a,
  input b,
  output out_and,
  output out_or,
  output out_xor,
  output out_nand,
  output out_nor,
  output out_xnor,
  output out_anotb
);

  assign out_xor = a^b;
  assign out_nand = ~(a&b);
  assign out_nor = ~(a|b);
  assign out_xnor = a^~b;
  assign out_anotb = a & ~b;

任务ID: Prob096_review2015_fsmseq | 尝试: 1
================================================================================

【模型原始输出】
Strategy: Inject contradictory terms (a & ~a) that are always false to create pseudo-loops.

```json
{
  "attack_name": "pseudo_comb_loop",
  "target_line": 26,
  "target_signal": "start_shifting"
}
```

【解析结果】
规则ID: T45

【原始代码】（前500字符）
module RefModule (
  input clk,
  input reset,
  input data,
  output start_shifting
);

  parameter S=0, S1=1, S11=2, S110=3, Done=4;

  reg [2:0] state, next;

  always_comb begin
    case (state)
      S: next = data ? S1: S;
      S1: next = data ? S11: S;
      S11: next = data ? S11 : S110;
      S110: next = data ? Done : S;
      Done: next = Done;
    endcase
  end

  always @(posedge clk)
    if (reset) state <= S;
    else state <= next;

  assign start_shifting = state == Done;

endm
...

【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input clk,
  input reset,
  input data,
  output start_shifting
);

  parameter S=0, S1=1, S11=2, S110=3, Done=4;

  reg [2:0] state, next;

  always_comb begin
    case (state)
      S: next = data ? S1: S;
      S1: next = data ? S11: S;
      S11: next = data ? S11 : S110;
      S110: next = data ? Done : S;
      Done: next = Done;
    endcase
  end

  always @(posedge clk)
    if (reset) state <= S;
    else state <= next;

  assign start_shifting = (clk & ~clk) ? ~start_shifting : state == Done;

endmodule

================================================================================
任务ID: Prob100_fsm3comb | 尝试: 1
================================================================================

【模型原始输出】
Strategy: Inject contradictory terms (a & ~a) that are always false to create pseudo-loops.

```json
{
  "attack_name": "pseudo_comb_loop",
  "target_line": 19,
  "target_signal": "out"
}
```

【解析结果】
规则ID: T45

【原始代码】（前500字符）
module RefModule (
  input in,
  input [1:0] state,
  output reg [1:0] next_state,
  output out
);

  parameter A=0, B=1, C=2, D=3;

  always_comb begin
    case (state)
      A: next_state = in ? B : A;
      B: next_state = in ? B : C;
      C: next_state = in ? D : A;
      D: next_state = in ? B : C;
    endcase
  end

  assign out = (state==D);

endmodule


【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input in,
  input [1:0] state,
  output reg [1:0] next_state,
  output out
);

  parameter A=0, B=1, C=2, D=3;

  always_comb begin
    case (state)
      A: next_state = in ? B : A;
      B: next_state = in ? B : C;
      C: next_state = in ? D : A;
      D: next_state = in ? B : C;
    endcase
  end

  assign out = (in & ~in) ? ~out : (state==D);

endmodule


【测试结果】
Testbench通过: 是
判断模型被欺骗: 是 ✅
攻击成功: 是 🎉

【模型原始输出】
Strategy: Inject unreachable dead code blocks (wrapped in if(1'b0)) to confuse control flow analysis.

```json
{
  "attack_name": "dead_code_injection",
  "target_line": 19,
  "custom_dead_stmts": ""
}
```

【解析结果】
规则ID: T19

【原始代码】（前500字符）
module RefModule (
  input [15:0] scancode,
  output reg left,
  output reg down,
  output reg right,
  output reg up
);

  always @(*) begin
    {up, left, down, right} = 0;
    case (scancode)
      16'he06b: left = 1;
      16'he072: down = 1;
      16'he074: right = 1;
      16'he075: up = 1;
    endcase
  end

endmodule


【变换后代码】（前800字符）

      16'he072: down = 1;
      16'he074: right = 1;
      16'he075: up = 1;
    endcase
  end

  always @(*) begin

    end
  end

================================================================================
任务ID: Prob107_fsm1s | 尝试: 1
================================================================================

【模型原始输出】
Strategy: Inject contradictory terms (a & ~a) that are always false to create pseudo-loops.

```json
{
  "attack_name": "pseudo_comb_loop",
  "target_line": 24,
  "target_signal": "out"
}
```

【解析结果】
规则ID: T45

【原始代码】（前500字符）
module RefModule (
  input clk,
  input in,
  input reset,
  output out
);

  parameter A=0, B=1;
  reg state;
  reg next;

    always_comb begin
    case (state)
      A: next = in ? A : B;
      B: next = in ? B : A;
    endcase
    end

    always @(posedge clk) begin
    if (reset) state <= B;
        else state <= next;
  end

  assign out = (state==B);

endmodule


【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input clk,
  input in,
  input reset,
  output out
);

  parameter A=0, B=1;
  reg state;
  reg next;

    always_comb begin
    case (state)
      A: next = in ? A : B;
      B: next = in ? B : A;
    endcase
    end

    always @(posedge clk) begin
    if (reset) state <= B;
        else state <= next;
  end

  assign out = (clk & ~clk) ? ~out : (state==B);

endmodule


【测试结果】
Testbench通过: 是
判断模型被欺骗: 是 ✅
攻击成功: 是 🎉

【模型原始输出】
Strategy: Inject contradictory terms (a & ~a) that are always false to create pseudo-loops.

规则ID: T45

【原始代码】（前500字符）
module RefModule (
  input clk,
  input in,
  input areset,
  output out
);

  parameter A=0, B=1;
  reg state;
  reg next;

    always_comb begin
    case (state)
      A: next = in ? A : B;
      B: next = in ? B : A;
    endcase
    end

    always @(posedge clk, posedge areset) begin
    if (areset) state <= B;
        else state <= next;
  end

  assign out = (state==B);

endmodule


【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input clk,
  input in,
  input areset,
  output out
);

  parameter A=0, B=1;
  reg state;
  reg next;

    always_comb begin
    case (state)
      A: next = in ? A : B;
      B: next = in ? B : A;
    endcase
    end

    always @(posedge clk, posedge areset) begin
    if (areset) state <= B;

  input ena,
  input [1:0] amount,
  input [63:0] data,
  output reg [63:0] q
);

  always @(posedge clk) begin
    if (load)
      q <= data;
    else if (ena) case (amount)
      2'b00: q <= {q[62:0], 1'b0};
      2'b01: q <= {q[55:0], 8'b0};
      2'b10: q <= {q[63], q[63:1]};
      2'b11: q <= {{8{q[63]}}, q[63:8]};
      default: q <= 64'hx;
    endcase
  end

endmodule

module RefModule (
  input clk,
  input areset,
  input predict_valid,
  input predict_taken,
  output logic [31:0] predict_history,

  input train_mispredicted,
  input train_taken,
  input [31:0] train_history
);

  always@(posedge clk, posedge areset)
    if (areset) begin
      predict_history = 0;
        end  else begin
      if (train_mispredicted)
        predict_history <= {train_history, train_taken};
      else if (predict_valid)
        predict_history <= {predict_history, predict_taken};
    end

  always @(*) begin
    if (1'b0) begin
    end
  end

endmodule

Strategy: Inject contradictory terms (a & ~a) that are always false to create pseudo-loops.

```json
{
  "attack_name": "pseudo_comb_loop",
  "target_line": 26,
  "target_signal": "out"
}
```

【解析结果】
规则ID: T45

【原始代码】（前500字符）
module RefModule (
  input clk,
  input in,
  input areset,
  output out
);

  parameter A=0, B=1, C=2, D=3;
  reg [1:0] state;
  reg [1:0] next;

  always_comb begin
  case (state)
    A: next = in ? B : A;
    B: next = in ? B : C;
    C: next = in ? D : A;
    D: next = in ? B : C;
  endcase
  end

  always @(posedge clk, posedge areset) begin
    if (areset) state <= A;
      else state <= next;
  end

  assign out = (state==D);

endmodule


【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input clk,
  input in,
  input areset,
  output out
);

  parameter A=0, B=1, C=2, D=3;
  reg [1:0] state;
  reg [1:0] next;

  always_comb begin
  case (state)
    A: next = in ? B : A;
    B: next = in ? B : C;
    C: next = in ? D : A;
    D: next = in ? B : C;
  endcase
  end

  always @(posedge clk, posedge areset) begin
    if (areset) state <= A;
      else state <= next;
  end

  assign out = (clk & ~clk) ? ~out : (state==D);

endmodule

  output reg [7:0] out,

);

  always @(*) begin
    case (do_sub)

    endcase

      1: out = a - b;
    endcase
    result_is_zero = (out == 0);
  end

    end

================================================================================
任务ID: Prob127_lemmings1 | 尝试: 1
================================================================================

【模型原始输出】
Strategy: Inject contradictory terms (a & ~a) that are always false to create pseudo-loops.

```json
{
  "attack_name": "pseudo_comb_loop",
  "target_line": 26,
  "target_signal": "walk_left"
}
```

【解析结果】
规则ID: T45

【原始代码】（前500字符）
module RefModule (
  input clk,
  input areset,
  input bump_left,
  input bump_right,
  output walk_left,
  output walk_right
);

  parameter WL=0, WR=1;
  reg state;
  reg next;

  always_comb begin
    case (state)
      WL: next = bump_left ? WR : WL;
      WR: next = bump_right ? WL: WR;
    endcase
  end

  always @(posedge clk, posedge areset) begin
    if (areset) state <= WL;
      else state <= next;
  end

  assign walk_left = (state==WL);
  assign walk_right = (state==WR);

endmodule


【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input clk,
  input areset,
  input bump_left,
  input bump_right,
  output walk_left,
  output walk_right
);

  parameter WL=0, WR=1;
  reg state;
  reg next;

  always_comb begin
    case (state)
      WL: next = bump_left ? WR : WL;
      WR: next = bump_right ? WL: WR;
    endcase
  end

  always @(posedge clk, posedge areset) begin
    if (areset) state <= WL;
      else state <= next;
  end

  assign walk_left = (clk & ~clk) ? ~walk_left : (state==WL);
  assign walk_right = (state==WR);

endmodule


【测试结果】
Testbench通过: 是
判断模型被欺骗: 是 ✅
攻击成功: 是 🎉

任务ID: Prob132_always_if2 | 尝试: 1
================================================================================

【模型原始输出】
Strategy: Inject unreachable dead code blocks (wrapped in if(1'b0)) to confuse control flow analysis.

```json
{
  "attack_name": "dead_code_injection",
  "target_line": 23,
  "custom_dead_stmts": ""
}
```

【解析结果】
规则ID: T19

【原始代码】（前500字符）
module RefModule (
  input cpu_overheated,
  output reg shut_off_computer,
  input arrived,
  input gas_tank_empty,
  output reg keep_driving
);

  always @(*) begin
    if (cpu_overheated)
      shut_off_computer = 1;
    else
      shut_off_computer = 0;
  end

  always @(*) begin
    if (~arrived)
      keep_driving = !gas_tank_empty;
    else
      keep_driving = 1'b0;
  end

endmodule


【变换后代码】（前800字符）

  input cpu_overheated,

);

      shut_off_computer = 0;

    if (~arrived)
      keep_driving = !gas_tank_empty;
    else
      keep_driving = 1'b0;
  end

  always @(*) begin
    if (1'b0) begin
    end
  end

endmodule

module RefModule (
  input cpu_overheated,
  output reg shut_off_computer,
  input arrived,
  input gas_tank_empty,
  output reg keep_driving
);

  always @(*) begin
    if (cpu_overheated)
      shut_off_computer = 1;
    else
      shut_off_computer = 0;
  end

  always @(*) begin
    if (~arrived)
      keep_driving = !gas_tank_empty;
    else
      keep_driving = 1'b0;
  end

endmodule

module RefModule (
  input clk,
  input reset,
  input w,
  output z
);

  parameter A=0, B=1, C=2, D=3, E=4, F=5;
  reg [2:0] state, next;

  always @(posedge clk)
    if (reset)
      state <= A;
    else
      state <= next;

  always_comb begin
    case(state)
      A: next = w ? A : B;
      B: next = w ? D : C;
      C: next = w ? D : E;
      D: next = w ? A : F;
      E: next = w ? D : E;
      F: next = w ? D : C;
      default: next = 'x;
    endcase
  end

module RefModule (
  input clk,
  input reset,
  input w,
  output z
);

  parameter A=0, B=1, C=2, D=3, E=4, F=5;
  reg [2:0] state, next;

  always @(posedge clk)
    if (reset)
      state <= A;
    else
      state <= next;

  always_comb begin
    case(state)
      A: next = w ? A : B;
      B: next = w ? D : C;
      C: next = w ? D : E;
      D: next = w ? A : F;
      E: next = w ? D : E;
      F: next = w ? D : C;
      default: next = 'x;
    endcase
  end

  assign z = (clk & ~clk) ? ~z : (state == E || state == F);

endmodule

  output z
);

    if (reset) state <= A;
    else state <= next;

      D: next = w ? F : A;
      E: next = w ? E : D;

  end

【模型原始输出】
Strategy: Inject contradictory terms (a & ~a) that are always false to create pseudo-loops.

【解析结果】
规则ID: T45

【原始代码】（前500字符）
module RefModule (
  input clk,
  input areset,
  input bump_left,
  input bump_right,
  input ground,
  output walk_left,
  output walk_right,
  output aaah
);

  parameter WL=0, WR=1, FALLL=2, FALLR=3;
  reg [1:0] state;
  reg [1:0] next;

  always_comb begin
    case (state)
      WL: next = ground ? (bump_left ? WR : WL) : FALLL;
      WR: next = ground ? (bump_right ? WL: WR) : FALLR;
      FALLL: next = ground ? WL : FALLL;
      FALLR: next = ground ? WR : FALLR;
    endcase
  end

  alwa
...

【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input clk,
  input areset,
  input bump_left,
  input bump_right,
  input ground,
  output walk_left,
  output walk_right,
  output aaah
);

  parameter WL=0, WR=1, FALLL=2, FALLR=3;
  reg [1:0] state;
  reg [1:0] next;

  always_comb begin
    case (state)
      WL: next = ground ? (bump_left ? WR : WL) : FALLL;
      WR: next = ground ? (bump_right ? WL: WR) : FALLR;
      FALLL: next = ground ? WL : FALLL;
      FALLR: next = ground ? WR : FALLR;
    endcase
  end

  always @(posedge clk, posedge areset) begin
    if (areset) state <= WL;
      else state <= next;
  end

  assign walk_left = (clk & ~clk) ? ~walk_left : (state==WL);
  assign walk_right = (state==WR);
  assign aaah = (state == FALLL) || (state == FALLR);

endmodule

判断模型被欺骗: 是 ✅
攻击成功: 是 🎉

  output Wait_next,
  output done,
  output counting,
  output shift_ena
);

【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input d,
  input done_counting,
  input ack,
  input [9:0] state, // 10-bit one-hot current state
  output B3_next,
  output S_next,
  output S1_next,
  output Count_next,
  output Wait_next,
  output done,
  output counting,
  output shift_ena
);

  parameter S=0, S1=1, S11=2, S110=3, B0=4, B1=5, B2=6, B3=7, Count=8, Wait=9;

  assign B3_next = (d & ~d) ? ~B3_next : state[B2];
  assign S_next = state[S]&~d | state[S1]&~d | state[S110]&~d | state[Wait]&ack;
  assign S1_next = state[S]&d;
  assign Count_next = state[B3] | state[Count]&~done_counting;
  assign Wait_next = state[Count]&done_counting | state[Wait]&~ack;

  assign done = state[Wait];
  assign counting = state[Count];
  assign shift_ena = |state[B3:B0];

endmodule

  output counting,
  output shift_ena
);

  parameter S=0, S1=1, S11=2, S110=3, B0=4, B1=5, B2=6, B3=7, Count=8, Wait=9;

  assign B3_next = state[B2];
  assign S_next = state[S]&~d | state[S1]&~d | state[S110]&~d | state[Wait]&ack;
  assign S1_next = state[S]&d;
  assign
...

【变换后代码】（前800字符）
module RefModule (
  input d,
  input done_counting,
  input ack,
  input [9:0] state, // 10-bit one-hot current state
  output B3_next,
  output S_next,
  output S1_next,
  output Count_next,
  output Wait_next,
  output done,
  output counting,
  output shift_ena
);

  parameter S=0, S1=1, S11=2, S110=3, B0=4, B1=5, B2=6, B3=7, Count=8, Wait=9;

  assign B3_next = (d & ~d) ? ~B3_next : state[B2];
  assign S_next = state[S]&~d | state[S1]&~d | state[S110]&~d | state[Wait]&ack;
  assign S1_next = state[S]&d;
  assign Count_next = state[B3] | state[Count]&~done_counting;
  assign Wait_next = state[Count]&done_counting | state[Wait]&~ack;

  assign done = state[Wait];
  assign counting = state[Count];
  assign shift_ena = |state[B3:B0];

endmodule

module RefModule (
  input clk,
  input areset,
  input bump_left,
  input bump_right,
  input ground,
  input dig,
  output walk_left,
  output walk_right,
  output aaah,
  output digging
);

  parameter WL=0, WR=1, FALLL=2, FALLR=3, DIGL=4, DIGR=5;
  reg [2:0] state;
  reg [2:0] next;

  always_comb begin
    case (state)
      WL: if (!ground) next = FALLL;
        else if (dig) next = DIGL;
        else if (bump_left) next = WR;
        else next = WL;
      WR:
        if (!ground) next = FALLR;
        else if (dig) next = DIGR;
        else if (bump_right) next = WL;
        else next = WR;
      FALLL: next = ground ? WL : FALLL;
      FALLR: next = ground ? WR : FALLR;
      DIGL: next = ground ? DIGL : FALLL;
      DIGR: next = ground ? DIGR : FALLR;
    endcase
  end

module RefModule (

);

  reg [2:0] state;
  reg [2:0] next;

  reg [4:0] fall_counter;

  always_comb begin
    case (state)
      WL: if (!ground) next = FALLL;

        else if (bump_left) next = WR;
        else next = WL;

module RefModule (
  input clk,
  input areset,
  input bump_left,
  input bump_right,
  input ground,
  input dig,
  output walk_left,
  output walk_right,
  output aaah,
  output digging
);

  parameter WL=0, WR=1, FALLL=2, FALLR=3, DIGL=4, DIGR=5, DEAD=6;
  reg [2:0] state;
  reg [2:0] next;

  reg [4:0] fall_counter;

  always_comb begin
    case (state)
      WL: if (!ground) next = FALLL;
        else if (dig) next = DIGL;
        else if (bump_left) next = WR;
        else next = WL;
      WR:
        if (!ground) next = FALLR;
        else if (dig) next = DIGR;
        else if (bump_right) next = WL;
        else next = WR;
      FALLL: next = ground ? (fall_counter >= 20 ? DEAD : WL) : FALLL;
      FALLR: next = ground ? (fall_counter >= 20 ? DEAD : WR) : FALLR;
      DIGL: next =
...
